<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbintenis.html>verbintenis</a> (9196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verbintenisse</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbinden.html>verbinden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verderfelijk.html>verderfelijk</a> (58776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verderflijc</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verderven.html>verderven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verderfelijk.html>verderfelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verderfelijk.html>verderfelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">verderfelijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deleterious, pernicious</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> putrefiable, nondurable</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a> (2209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verdiepinge</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepen.html>verdiepen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepingen.html>verdiepingen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdiepinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>deepening</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:floor.html>floor</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:storey.html>storey</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage <a href = vnd.unilang:notes.html>notes</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>In</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Dutch-speaking countries, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>first</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:floor.html>floor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:floor.html>floor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:level.html>level</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:above.html>above</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ground.html>ground</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:level.html>level</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ground.html>ground</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:floor.html>floor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begane.html>begane</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:until.html>Until</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> seventeenth <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:could.html>could</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mean.html>mean</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:both.html>both</a> “ground floor” <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> “first floor”.
